1. Create/list/delete agents in the mimo-platform (not start them)

   - Click to show agent details

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/mimo-platform/specs/agent-lifecycle/spec.md

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 00:18:54
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/mimo-platform/specs/agent-lifecycle/spec.md

```
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/mimo-platform/specs/agent-lifecycle/spec.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: ## ADDED Requirements
2: 
3: ### Requirement: User can create an agent
4: The system SHALL allow users to create agents for sessions. Creating an agent generates a token and spawns mimo-agent process.
5: 
6: #### Scenario: Create agent for session
7: - **WHEN** authenticated user creates agent for session "fix-auth-bug"
8: - **THEN** system generates JWT token {session_id: "...", exp: "..."}
9: - **AND** system spawns mimo-agent process with --token=<jwt> --platform=ws://localhost:4000/agent
10: - **AND** system stores agent.yaml with {token: "...", session_id: "...", status: "starting"}
11: - **AND** system displays "Agent starting..." in chat buffer
12: 
13: #### Scenario: Agent connects successfully
14: - **WHEN** mimo-agent connects via WebSocket with valid token
15: - **THEN** system updates agent.yaml status to "connected"
16: - **AND** system appends "Agent connected" to chat buffer
17: 
18: #### Scenario: Agent fails to start
19: - **WHEN** mimo-agent executable not found or crashes
20: - **THEN** system updates agent.yaml status to "failed"
21: - **AND** system displays error message in chat buffer
22: - **AND** system allows retry
23: 
24: ### Requirement: User can list active agents
25: The system SHALL display running agents for the current user.
26: 
27: #### Scenario: List active agents
28: - **WHEN** user navigates to agents page
29: - **THEN** system displays all agents with status: session name, status, pid, started_at
30: 
31: #### Scenario: Filter by status
32: - **WHEN** user filters agents by "connected" status
33: - **THEN** system displays only agents with status "connected"
34: 
35: ### Requirement: System can cancel current ACP request
36: The system SHALL allow users to cancel the current ACP agent request.
37: 
38: #### Scenario: Cancel current request with C-c C-c
39: - **WHEN** user presses C-c C-c in session
40: - **THEN** system sends cancel signal to current ACP request
41: - **AND** system appends "Request cancelled" to chat buffer
42: - **AND** agent remains connected and ready for next request
43: 
44: #### Scenario: Cancel when no active request
45: - **WHEN** user presses C-c C-c with no active ACP request
46: - **THEN** system displays "No active request to cancel"
47: 
48: ### Requirement: System can terminate agent
49: The system SHALL allow users to kill the entire agent process.
50: 
51: #### Scenario: Kill agent via command
52: - **WHEN** user executes kill-agent command
53: - **THEN** system terminates mimo-agent process
54: - **AND** system kills ACP child process
55: - **AND** system updates agent.yaml status to "killed"
56: - **AND** system appends "Agent terminated" to chat buffer
57: 
58: #### Scenario: Agent process dies unexpectedly
59: - **WHEN** mimo-agent process exits unexpectedly
60: - **THEN** system detects via WebSocket disconnect
61: - **AND** system kills any orphaned ACP process
62: - **AND** system updates agent.yaml status to "died"
63: 
64: ### Requirement: Agent persists across disconnects
65: The system SHALL maintain agent process when user disconnects.
66: 
67: #### Scenario: Agent continues after disconnect
68: - **WHEN** user disconnects from session
69: - **THEN** mimo-agent process continues running
70: - **AND** agent continues working on assigned tasks
71: 
72: #### Scenario: Agent reports changes after reconnect
73: - **WHEN** user reconnects after agent made file changes
74: - **THEN** system receives buffered change notifications
75: - **AND** system updates file tree with changes
76: 
77: ### Requirement: Agent uses token for authentication
78: The system SHALL validate JWT tokens from agents.
79: 
80: #### Scenario: Valid token authentication
81: - **WHEN** agent connects with valid JWT token
82: - **THEN** system identifies session from token claims
83: - **AND** system authorizes WebSocket connection
84: 
85: #### Scenario: Invalid token rejection
86: - **WHEN** agent connects with invalid or expired token
87: - **THEN** system rejects WebSocket connection
88: - **AND** system logs authentication failure

(End of file - total 88 lines)
</content>
```

<type>file</type>
<content>1: ## ADDED Requirements
2: 
3: ### Requirement: User can create a session
4: The system SHALL allow users to create sessions within a project. Each session creates a worktree and starts a Fossil server.
5: 
6: #### Scenario: Create session with title
7: - **WHEN** authenticated user submits session title "fix-auth-bug" for project "my-app"
8: - **THEN** system creates directory ~/.mimo/projects/my-app/sessions/fix-auth-bug/
9: - **AND** system clones project's repository to repo.fossil
10: - **AND** system assigns auto-generated port (8000-9000 range)
11: - **AND** system starts Fossil server on assigned port
12: - **AND** system stores session.yaml with {title: "fix-auth-bug", port: <assigned>, status: "active"}
13: - **AND** system displays session view
14: 
15: #### Scenario: Port collision handling
16: - **WHEN** system attempts to start Fossil server on occupied port
17: - **THEN** system tries next available port in range
18: - **AND** system continues until successful
19: 
20: #### Scenario: Duplicate session title
21: - **WHEN** user submits session title that already exists in project
22: - **THEN** system appends timestamp to title or returns error
23: 
24: ### Requirement: Session persists across disconnects
25: The system SHALL maintain session state when user disconnects.
26: 
27: #### Scenario: Reconnect to active session
28: - **WHEN** user reconnects to existing session
29: - **THEN** system loads chat history from messages.jsonl
30: - **AND** system reattaches to running agent if exists
31: - **AND** system displays current file tree state
32: 
33: #### Scenario: Agent running on reconnect
34: - **WHEN** user reconnects and agent is still running
35: - **THEN** system establishes WebSocket to agent
36: - **AND** system resumes chat stream
37: 
38: ### Requirement: User can delete a session
39: The system SHALL allow users to remove sessions.
40: 
41: #### Scenario: Delete session with cleanup
42: - **WHEN** authenticated user deletes session "fix-auth-bug"
43: - **THEN** system terminates agent process if running
44: - **AND** system stops Fossil server
45: - **AND** system removes ~/.mimo/projects/my-app/sessions/fix-auth-bug/ directory
46: 
47: ### Requirement: Chat messages are stored persistently
48: The system SHALL store chat history in append-only JSONL format.
49: 
50: #### Scenario: Store user message
51: - **WHEN** user sends message "Add dark mode"
52: - **THEN** system appends to messages.jsonl: {type: "user", content: "Add dark mode", timestamp: "..."}
53: 
54: #### Scenario: Store agent message
55: - **WHEN** agent sends response "I'll help with that..."
56: - **THEN** system appends to messages.jsonl: {type: "agent", content: "...", timestamp: "..."}
57: 
58: #### Scenario: Stream agent response
59: - **WHEN** agent streams response in chunks
60: - **THEN** system buffers and stores complete message on finish
61: - **AND** system displays streaming updates via WebSocket
62: 
63: ### Requirement: Session shows file tree with change indicators
64: The system SHALL display project file tree with modification markers in the left buffer.
65: 
66: #### Scenario: Show modified files
67: - **WHEN** agent reports file changes
68: - **THEN** system marks files with [M] in file tree (left buffer)
69: - **AND** system updates changes buffer (right buffer)
70: 
71: #### Scenario: Show new files
72: - **WHEN** agent creates new files
73: - **THEN** system marks files with [?] in file tree (left buffer)
74: 
75: ### Requirement: Session shows file diffs with syntax highlighting
76: The system SHALL display file changes with language-appropriate syntax highlighting.
77: 
78: #### Scenario: View file diff
79: - **WHEN** user clicks on modified file
80: - **THEN** system displays diff with syntax highlighting
81: - **AND** system shows line additions and deletions
82: 
83: ### Requirement: User can navigate file tree
84: The system SHALL allow users to browse and open files.
85: 
86: #### Scenario: Find file
87: - **WHEN** user presses the configured keybinding for find_file
88: - **THEN** system prompts for file path
89: - **AND** system opens file in file buffer
90: 
91: #### Scenario: Click file in tree
92: - **WHEN** user clicks file in file tree
93: - **THEN** system loads file content into file buffer
94: 
95: ### Requirement: Keybindings are configurable
96: The system SHALL allow users to customize keybindings stored in ~/.mimo/config.yaml.
97: 
98: #### Scenario: Load custom keybindings
99: - **WHEN** user starts platform
100: - **THEN** system reads ~/.mimo/config.yaml
101: - **AND** system loads custom keybindings if defined
102: - **AND** system uses defaults for missing bindings
103: 
104: #### Scenario: Use default keybinding
105: - **WHEN** user presses C-c C-c (default cancel)
106: - **THEN** system executes cancel agent command
107: - **AND** keybinding is configurable via config.yaml
108: 
109: #### Scenario: Focus buffer with keybinding
110: - **WHEN** user presses C-x h
111: - **THEN** system focuses file buffer (left)
112: - **AND** system updates active buffer indicator
113: 
114: #### Scenario: Focus chat buffer
115: - **WHEN** user presses C-x j
116: - **THEN** system focuses chat buffer (center)
117: - **AND** system updates active buffer indicator
118: 
119: #### Scenario: Focus changes buffer
120: - **WHEN** user presses C-x l
121: - **THEN** system focuses changes buffer (right)
122: - **AND** system updates active buffer indicator

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/agents/service.ts

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 00:18:56

```
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/agents/service.ts</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: import { spawn, Subprocess } from "bun";
2: import { join } from "path";
3: import { Agent, AgentRepository, AgentStatus, agentRepository } from "./repository.js";
4: import { ChatService, chatService } from "../sessions/chat.js";
5: import { SignJWT, jwtVerify } from "jose";
6: import { getPaths } from "../config/paths.js";
7: 
8: const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET || "your-secret-key-change-in-production";
9: const AGENT_SECRET = new TextEncoder().encode(JWT_SECRET);
10: const PLATFORM_URL = process.env.PLATFORM_URL || "ws://localhost:3000";
11: 
12: export interface AgentTokenPayload {
13:   agentId: string;
14:   sessionId: string;
15:   projectId: string;
16:   owner: string;
17: }
18: 
19: export interface SpawnAgentInput {
20:   sessionId: string;
21:   projectId: string;
22:   owner: string;
23:   agentPath?: string; // Path to mimo-agent binary
24: }
25: 
26: export class AgentService {
27:   private runningProcesses: Map<string, Subprocess> = new Map();
28:   private activeConnections: Map<string, WebSocket> = new Map();
29:   private currentAcpRequest: Map<string, AbortController> = new Map();
30: 
31:   constructor(
32:     private repository: AgentRepository = agentRepository,
33:     private chat: ChatService = chatService
34:   ) {}
35: 
36:   async generateAgentToken(agent: Agent): Promise<string> {
37:     const token = await new SignJWT({
38:       agentId: agent.id,
39:       sessionId: agent.sessionId,
40:       projectId: agent.projectId,
41:       owner: agent.owner,
42:     })
43:       .setProtectedHeader({ alg: "HS256" })
44:       .setIssuedAt()
45:       .setExpirationTime("24h")
46:       .sign(AGENT_SECRET);
47: 
48:     return token;
49:   }
50: 
51:   async verifyAgentToken(token: string): Promise<AgentTokenPayload | null> {
52:     try {
53:       const { payload } = await jwtVerify(token, AGENT_SECRET);
54:       return {
55:         agentId: payload.agentId as string,
56:         sessionId: payload.sessionId as string,
57:         projectId: payload.projectId as string,
58:         owner: payload.owner as string,
59:       };
60:     } catch {
61:       return null;
62:     }
63:   }
64: 
65:   async spawnAgent(input: SpawnAgentInput): Promise<Agent> {
66:     // Generate token first
67:     const tempToken = await new SignJWT({
68:       sessionId: input.sessionId,
69:       projectId: input.projectId,
70:       owner: input.owner,
71:     })
72:       .setProtectedHeader({ alg: "HS256" })
73:       .setIssuedAt()
74:       .setExpirationTime("24h")
75:       .sign(AGENT_SECRET);
76: 
77:     // Create agent record
78:     const agent = await this.repository.create({
79:       sessionId: input.sessionId,
80:       projectId: input.projectId,
81:       owner: input.owner,
82:       token: tempToken,
83:     });
84: 
85:     // Generate proper token with agent ID
86:     const token = await this.generateAgentToken(agent);
87:     await this.repository.update(agent.id, { token });
88:     agent.token = token;
89: 
90:     // Add system message
91:     await this.chat.saveMessage(input.sessionId, {
92:       role: "system",
93:       content: "Agent starting...",
94:       timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
95:       metadata: { agentId: agent.id },
96:     });
97: 
98:     // Try to spawn the agent process
99:     try {
100:       await this.startAgentProcess(agent, input.agentPath);
101:     } catch (error) {
102:       await this.handleAgentFailure(agent.id, error as Error);
103:       throw error;
104:     }
105: 
106:     return agent;
107:   }
108: 
109:   private async startAgentProcess(agent: Agent, agentPath?: string): Promise<void> {
110:     const binary = agentPath || process.env.MIMO_AGENT_PATH || "mimo-agent";
111:     const platformWsUrl = `${PLATFORM_URL}/ws/agent`;
112: 
113:     try {
114:       const proc = spawn({
115:         cmd: [binary, "--token", agent.token, "--platform", platformWsUrl],
116:         stdout: "pipe",
117:         stderr: "pipe",
118:         onExit: async (code, signal) => {
119:           await this.handleProcessExit(agent.id, code, signal);
120:         },
121:       });
122: 
123:       this.runningProcesses.set(agent.id, proc);
124: 
125:       // Update agent with PID
126:       if (proc.pid) {
127:         await this.repository.updatePid(agent.id, proc.pid);
128:       }
129: 
130:       // Monitor stderr for errors
131:       if (proc.stderr) {
132:         const reader = proc.stderr.getReader();
133:         (async () => {
134:           try {
135:             while (true) {
136:               const { done, value } = await reader.read();
137:               if (done) break;
138:               const errorText = new TextDecoder().decode(value);
139:               console.error(`Agent ${agent.id} stderr:`, errorText);
140:             }
141:           } catch (error) {
142:             console.error(`Error reading agent ${agent.id} stderr:`, error);
143:           }
144:         })();
145:       }
146:     } catch (error) {
147:       throw new Error(`Failed to spawn agent process: ${(error as Error).message}`);
148:     }
149:   }
150: 
151:   private async handleProcessExit(
152:     agentId: string, 
153:     code: number | null, 
154:     signal: number | null
155:   ): Promise<void> {
156:     const agent = await this.repository.findById(agentId);
157:     if (!agent) return;
158: 
159:     // Remove from running processes
160:     this.runningProcesses.delete(agentId);
161:     this.activeConnections.delete(agentId);
162:     this.currentAcpRequest.delete(agentId);
163: 
164:     if (code === 0 || signal === 0) {
165:       // Normal exit - already handled by kill command
166:       return;
167:     }
168: 
169:     // Unexpected exit
170:     const status: AgentStatus = agent.status === "killed" ? "killed" : "died";
171:     await this.repository.updateStatus(agentId, status);
172: 
173:     // Clean up orphaned ACP processes if any
174:     if (agent.pid) {
175:       try {
176:         process.kill(agent.pid, 0); // Check if process exists
177:         process.kill(agent.pid, "SIGTERM");
178:       } catch {
179:         // Process already gone
180:       }
181:     }
182: 
183:     // Notify via chat
184:     await this.chat.saveMessage(agent.sessionId, {
185:       role: "system",
186:       content: status === "killed" 
187:         ? "Agent terminated" 
188:         : `Agent process died unexpectedly (code: ${code}, signal: ${signal})`,
189:       timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
190:       metadata: { agentId, code, signal },
191:     });
192:   }
193: 
194:   private async handleAgentFailure(agentId: string, error: Error): Promise<void> {
195:     await this.repository.updateStatus(agentId, "failed");
196: 
197:     const agent = await this.repository.findById(agentId);
198:     if (agent) {
199:       await this.chat.saveMessage(agent.sessionId, {
200:         role: "system",
201:         content: `Agent failed to start: ${error.message}`,
202:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
203:         metadata: { agentId, error: error.message },
204:       });
205:     }
206:   }
207: 
208:   async handleAgentConnect(agentId: string, ws: WebSocket): Promise<void> {
209:     const agent = await this.repository.findById(agentId);
210:     if (!agent) {
211:       ws.close(1008, "Agent not found");
212:       return;
213:     }
214: 
215:     this.activeConnections.set(agentId, ws);
216:     await this.repository.updateStatus(agentId, "connected");
217:     await this.repository.updateLastActivity(agentId);
218: 
219:     await this.chat.saveMessage(agent.sessionId, {
220:       role: "system",
221:       content: "Agent connected",
222:       timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
223:       metadata: { agentId },
224:     });
225:   }
226: 
227:   async handleAgentDisconnect(agentId: string): Promise<void> {
228:     this.activeConnections.delete(agentId);
229:     
230:     const agent = await this.repository.findById(agentId);
231:     if (agent && agent.status === "connected") {
232:       await this.repository.updateStatus(agentId, "died");
233:       
234:       await this.chat.saveMessage(agent.sessionId, {
235:         role: "system",
236:         content: "Agent disconnected unexpectedly",
237:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
238:         metadata: { agentId },
239:       });
240:     }
241:   }
242: 
243:   async cancelCurrentRequest(sessionId: string): Promise<boolean> {
244:     const agents = await this.repository.findBySessionId(sessionId);
245:     const connectedAgent = agents.find(a => a.status === "connected");
246:     
247:     if (!connectedAgent) {
248:       await this.chat.saveMessage(sessionId, {
249:         role: "system",
250:         content: "No active request to cancel",
251:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
252:       });
253:       return false;
254:     }
255: 
256:     const controller = this.currentAcpRequest.get(connectedAgent.id);
257:     if (controller) {
258:       controller.abort();
259:       this.currentAcpRequest.delete(connectedAgent.id);
260:     }
261: 
262:     // Send cancel message via WebSocket
263:     const ws = this.activeConnections.get(connectedAgent.id);
264:     if (ws) {
265:       ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: "cancel_request" }));
266:     }
267: 
268:     await this.chat.saveMessage(sessionId, {
269:       role: "system",
270:       content: "Request cancelled",
271:       timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
272:       metadata: { agentId: connectedAgent.id },
273:     });
274: 
275:     return true;
276:   }
277: 
278:   async killAgent(agentId: string): Promise<boolean> {
279:     const agent = await this.repository.findById(agentId);
280:     if (!agent) return false;
281: 
282:     // Send kill command via WebSocket first
283:     const ws = this.activeConnections.get(agentId);
284:     if (ws) {
285:       ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: "terminate" }));
286:       ws.close(1000, "Agent terminated by user");
287:     }
288: 
289:     // Kill the process
290:     const proc = this.runningProcesses.get(agentId);
291:     if (proc) {
292:       proc.kill();
293:       this.runningProcesses.delete(agentId);
294:     }
295: 
296:     // If process kill didn't work, try direct signal
297:     if (agent.pid) {
298:       try {
299:         process.kill(agent.pid, "SIGTERM");
300:         setTimeout(() => {
301:           try {
302:             process.kill(agent.pid!, "SIGKILL");
303:           } catch {
304:             // Already dead
305:           }
306:         }, 5000);
307:       } catch {
308:         // Already dead
309:       }
310:     }
311: 
312:     await this.repository.updateStatus(agentId, "killed");
313:     this.activeConnections.delete(agentId);
314:     this.currentAcpRequest.delete(agentId);
315: 
316:     await this.chat.saveMessage(agent.sessionId, {
317:       role: "system",
318:       content: "Agent terminated",
319:       timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
320:       metadata: { agentId },
321:     });
322: 
323:     return true;
324:   }
325: 
326:   async killAgentsBySession(sessionId: string): Promise<number> {
327:     const agents = await this.repository.findBySessionId(sessionId);
328:     let killed = 0;
329: 
330:     for (const agent of agents) {
331:       if (agent.status === "connected" || agent.status === "starting") {
332:         await this.killAgent(agent.id);
333:         killed++;
334:       }
335:     }
336: 
337:     return killed;
338:   }
339: 
340:   async getAgentStatus(agentId: string): Promise<Agent | null> {
341:     return this.repository.findById(agentId);
342:   }
343: 
344:   async listAgentsByOwner(owner: string): Promise<Agent[]> {
345:     return this.repository.findByOwner(owner);
346:   }
347: 
348:   async listAgentsBySession(sessionId: string): Promise<Agent[]> {
349:     return this.repository.findBySessionId(sessionId);
350:   }
351: 
352:   async cleanupDeadAgents(): Promise<void> {
353:     const Paths = getPaths();
354:     const agentsDir = Paths.agents;
355:     
356:     const { readdirSync, existsSync } = require("fs");
357:     if (!existsSync(agentsDir)) return;
358: 
359:     const entries = readdirSync(agentsDir, { withFileTypes: true });
360:     
361:     for (const entry of entries) {
362:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
363:         const agent = await this.repository.findById(entry.name);
364:         if (agent && agent.pid) {
365:           try {
366:             // Check if process still exists
367:             process.kill(agent.pid, 0);
368:           } catch {
369:             // Process is gone
370:             if (agent.status === "connected" || agent.status === "starting") {
371:               await this.repository.updateStatus(agent.id, "died");
372:             }
373:           }
374:         }
375:       }
376:     }
377:   }
378: 
379:   // Called when a new ACP request starts
380:   startAcpRequest(agentId: string): AbortController {
381:     const controller = new AbortController();
382:     this.currentAcpRequest.set(agentId, controller);
383:     return controller;
384:   }
385: 
386:   // Called when ACP request completes
387:   endAcpRequest(agentId: string): void {
388:     this.currentAcpRequest.delete(agentId);
389:   }
390: 
391:   // Send message to agent
392:   async sendToAgent(agentId: string, message: unknown): Promise<boolean> {
393:     const ws = this.activeConnections.get(agentId);
394:     if (!ws) return false;
395: 
396:     try {
397:       ws.send(JSON.stringify(message));
398:       return true;
399:     } catch {
400:       return false;
401:     }
402:   }
403: }
404: 
405: export const agentService = new AgentService();

207:   // Get session info for respawn
208:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(agent.sessionId);
209:   if (!session) {

214:   try {
215:     await agentService.spawnAgent({
216:       sessionId: agent.sessionId,
217:       projectId: agent.projectId,
218:       owner: username,
219:     });

221:     return c.text(`Failed to restart agent: ${(error as Error).message}`, 500);
222:   }
223: 
224:   return c.redirect("/agents");

<content>1: import { join } from "path";
2: import { existsSync, mkdirSync, writeFileSync, readFileSync, readdirSync, rmdirSync, unlinkSync } from "fs";
3: import { getPaths } from "../config/paths.js";
4: import { dump, load } from "js-yaml";
5: import crypto from "crypto";
6: 
7: export type AgentStatus = 
8:   | "starting" 
9:   | "connected" 
10:   | "failed" 
11:   | "killed" 
12:   | "died";
13: 
14: export interface Agent {
15:   id: string;
16:   sessionId: string;
17:   projectId: string;
18:   owner: string;
19:   token: string;
20:   status: AgentStatus;
21:   pid?: number;
22:   startedAt: Date;
23:   updatedAt: Date;
24:   lastActivityAt?: Date;
25: }
26: 
27: export interface AgentData {
28:   id: string;
29:   sessionId: string;
30:   projectId: string;
31:   owner: string;
32:   token: string;
33:   status: AgentStatus;
34:   pid?: number;
35:   startedAt: string;
36:   updatedAt: string;
37:   lastActivityAt?: string;
38: }
39: 
40: export interface CreateAgentInput {
41:   sessionId: string;
42:   projectId: string;
43:   owner: string;
44:   token: string;
45: }
46: 
47: export class AgentRepository {
48:   private getAgentPath(agentId: string): string {
49:     return join(getPaths().agents, agentId);
50:   }
51: 
52:   private getAgentFilePath(agentId: string): string {
53:     return join(this.getAgentPath(agentId), "agent.yaml");
54:   }
55: 
56:   private generateId(): string {
57:     return crypto.randomUUID();
58:   }
59: 
60:   async create(input: CreateAgentInput): Promise<Agent> {
61:     const id = this.generateId();
62:     const agentPath = this.getAgentPath(id);
63:     
64:     if (!existsSync(agentPath)) {
65:       mkdirSync(agentPath, { recursive: true });
66:     }
67: 
68:     const now = new Date().toISOString();
69:     const agentData: AgentData = {
70:       id,
71:       sessionId: input.sessionId,
72:       projectId: input.projectId,
73:       owner: input.owner,
74:       token: input.token,
75:       status: "starting",
76:       startedAt: now,
77:       updatedAt: now,
78:     };
79: 
80:     writeFileSync(this.getAgentFilePath(id), dump(agentData), "utf-8");
81: 
82:     return {
83:       ...agentData,
84:       startedAt: new Date(agentData.startedAt),
85:       updatedAt: new Date(agentData.updatedAt),
86:       lastActivityAt: agentData.lastActivityAt 
87:         ? new Date(agentData.lastActivityAt) 
88:         : undefined,
89:     };
90:   }
91: 
92:   async findById(agentId: string): Promise<Agent | null> {
93:     const filePath = this.getAgentFilePath(agentId);
94:     if (!existsSync(filePath)) {
95:       return null;
96:     }
97: 
98:     const content = readFileSync(filePath, "utf-8");
99:     const data = load(content) as AgentData;
100: 
101:     return {
102:       ...data,
103:       startedAt: new Date(data.startedAt),
104:       updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
105:       lastActivityAt: data.lastActivityAt 
106:         ? new Date(data.lastActivityAt) 
107:         : undefined,
108:     };
109:   }
110: 
111:   async findBySessionId(sessionId: string): Promise<Agent[]> {
112:     const Paths = getPaths();
113:     if (!existsSync(Paths.agents)) {
114:       return [];
115:     }
116: 
117:     const entries = readdirSync(Paths.agents, { withFileTypes: true });
118:     const agents: Agent[] = [];
119: 
120:     for (const entry of entries) {
121:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
122:         const agentFile = join(Paths.agents, entry.name, "agent.yaml");
123:         if (existsSync(agentFile)) {
124:           const content = readFileSync(agentFile, "utf-8");
125:           const data = load(content) as AgentData;
126:           if (data.sessionId === sessionId) {
127:             agents.push({
128:               ...data,
129:               startedAt: new Date(data.startedAt),
130:               updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
131:               lastActivityAt: data.lastActivityAt 
132:                 ? new Date(data.lastActivityAt) 
133:                 : undefined,
134:             });
135:           }
136:         }
137:       }
138:     }
139: 
140:     return agents.sort((a, b) => b.startedAt.getTime() - a.startedAt.getTime());
141:   }
142: 
143:   async findByOwner(owner: string): Promise<Agent[]> {
144:     const Paths = getPaths();
145:     if (!existsSync(Paths.agents)) {
146:       return [];
147:     }
148: 
149:     const entries = readdirSync(Paths.agents, { withFileTypes: true });
150:     const agents: Agent[] = [];
151: 
152:     for (const entry of entries) {
153:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
154:         const agentFile = join(Paths.agents, entry.name, "agent.yaml");
155:         if (existsSync(agentFile)) {
156:           const content = readFileSync(agentFile, "utf-8");
157:           const data = load(content) as AgentData;
158:           if (data.owner === owner) {
159:             agents.push({
160:               ...data,
161:               startedAt: new Date(data.startedAt),
162:               updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
163:               lastActivityAt: data.lastActivityAt 
164:                 ? new Date(data.lastActivityAt) 
165:                 : undefined,
166:             });
167:           }
168:         }
169:       }
170:     }
171: 
172:     return agents.sort((a, b) => b.startedAt.getTime() - a.startedAt.getTime());
173:   }
174: 
175:   async update(
176:     agentId: string, 
177:     updates: Partial<Omit<AgentData, "id" | "startedAt">>
178:   ): Promise<Agent | null> {
179:     const agent = await this.findById(agentId);
180:     if (!agent) return null;
181: 
182:     const updatedData: AgentData = {
183:       ...agent,
184:       ...updates,
185:       updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
186:     };
187: 
188:     const filePath = this.getAgentFilePath(agentId);
189:     writeFileSync(filePath, dump(updatedData), "utf-8");
190: 
191:     return {
192:       ...updatedData,
193:       startedAt: new Date(updatedData.startedAt),
194:       updatedAt: new Date(updatedData.updatedAt),
195:       lastActivityAt: updatedData.lastActivityAt 
196:         ? new Date(updatedData.lastActivityAt) 
197:         : undefined,
198:     };
199:   }
200: 
201:   async updateStatus(agentId: string, status: AgentStatus): Promise<Agent | null> {
202:     return this.update(agentId, { status });
203:   }
204: 
205:   async updatePid(agentId: string, pid: number): Promise<Agent | null> {
206:     return this.update(agentId, { pid });
207:   }
208: 
209:   async updateLastActivity(agentId: string): Promise<Agent | null> {
210:     return this.update(agentId, { lastActivityAt: new Date().toISOString() });
211:   }
212: 
213:   async delete(agentId: string): Promise<void> {
214:     const agentPath = this.getAgentPath(agentId);
215:     if (existsSync(agentPath)) {
216:       this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(agentPath);
217:     }
218:   }
219: 
220:   private deleteDirectoryRecursive(dirPath: string): void {
221:     if (!existsSync(dirPath)) return;
222: 
223:     const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
224:     
225:     for (const entry of entries) {
226:       const entryPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
227:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
228:         this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(entryPath);
229:       } else {
230:         unlinkSync(entryPath);
231:       }
232:     }
233: 
234:     rmdirSync(dirPath);
235:   }
236: 
237:   async exists(agentId: string): Promise<boolean> {
238:     return existsSync(this.getAgentFilePath(agentId));
239:   }
240: }
241: 
242: export const agentRepository = new AgentRepository();

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 00:18:58)

Now I understand the current agent lifecycle model clearly. Let me visualize what's happening and what the user wants:

**Current Model (what the user says is wrong):**
```
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                  MIMO-PLATFORM                       │
│                                                      │
│   ┌────────────┐      spawn         ┌─────────────┐ │
│   │   User     │ ──────────────────▶│   Agent     │ │
│   │            │                    │   Process   │ │
│   │            │                    │             │ │
│   │            │      manages       │  (mimo-     │ │
│   │            │ ◀─────────────────▶│   agent)    │ │
│   │            │     (WebSocket)    │             │ │
│   └────────────┘                    └─────────────┘ │
│                                                      │
│   "Start Agent" button                               │
│   - Platform spawns process                          │
│   - Platform manages lifecycle                       │
│   - Token generated FOR the agent                    │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**What the User Wants:**
```
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                  MIMO-PLATFORM                       │
│                                                      │
│   ┌────────────┐  create   ┌─────────────┐          │
│   │   User     │ ─────────▶│   Agent     │          │
│   │            │           │   Record    │          │
│   │            │           │   (token,    │          │
│   │            │           │    status)   │          │
│   │            │           └─────────────┘          │
│   │            │                 │                   │
│   │            │   display token │                   │
│   │            │ ◀───────────────┘                   │
│   │            │                                     │
│   │            │   ┌────────────┐                   │
│   │            │   │  Details   │                   │
│   │            │   │  Panel     │                   │
│   │            │   │  (online/  │                   │
│   │  click     │   │   offline) │                   │
│   │  status    │ ─▶│            │                   │
│   └────────────┘   └────────────┘                   │
│                                                      │
│   User spawns agent OUTSIDE platform:                │
│   mimo-agent --token=<jwt> --platform=ws://...      │
│                                                      │
│   Session indicates which agent created it          │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

Key changes:
1. **No "Start Agent" button** - Platform doesn't spawn the agent
2. **Create Agent** - Creates agent record + generates token
3. **Display Token** - User copies token to start agent themselves
4. **List Agents** - Shows all agents for user
5. **Agent Status** - Shows online/offline based on WebSocket connection
6. **Click Status** - Shows details panel (not start agent)
7. **Session-Agent Link** - When creating session, indicate which agent is associated

The user's insight is important: The platform should be **token-provider/registry**, not **process-manager**.

Let me explore more to understand the session-agent relationship and see the UI routes.
## Agent (2026-04-04 00:19:06)

Let me look at sessions and how they relate to agents:

43:   }
44: 
45:   private generateId(): string {
46:     return crypto.randomUUID();
47:   }
48: 
49:   private getWorktreePath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {
50:     return join(getPaths().projects, projectId, "worktrees", sessionId);
51:   }
52: 
53:   async create(input: CreateSessionInput): Promise<Session> {
54:     const id = this.generateId();
55:     const sessionPath = this.getSessionPath(input.projectId, id);
56:     const worktreePath = this.getWorktreePath(input.projectId, id);
57:     
58:     // Create session directory
59:     if (!existsSync(sessionPath)) {
60:       mkdirSync(sessionPath, { recursive: true });
61:     }
62: 
63:     // Create worktree directory
64:     if (!existsSync(worktreePath)) {
65:       mkdirSync(worktreePath, { recursive: true });
66:     }
67: 
68:     const now = new Date().toISOString();
69:     const sessionData: SessionData = {
70:       id,
71:       name: input.name,
72:       projectId: input.projectId,
73:       owner: input.owner,
74:       worktreePath,
75:       status: "active",
76:       createdAt: now,
77:       updatedAt: now,
78:     };
79: 
80:     writeFileSync(
81:       this.getSessionFilePath(input.projectId, id),
82:       dump(sessionData),
83:       "utf-8"
84:     );
85: 
86:     return {
87:       ...sessionData,
88:       createdAt: new Date(sessionData.createdAt),
89:       updatedAt: new Date(sessionData.updatedAt),
90:     };
91:   }
92: 
93:   async findById(sessionId: string): Promise<Session | null> {
94:     // Search across all projects for the session
95:     const Paths = getPaths();
96:     if (!existsSync(Paths.projects)) {
97:       return null;
98:     }
99: 
100:     const projectEntries = readdirSync(Paths.projects, { withFileTypes: true });
101:     
102:     for (const projectEntry of projectEntries) {
103:       if (projectEntry.isDirectory()) {
104:         const sessionsDir = join(Paths.projects, projectEntry.name, "sessions");
105:         if (existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
106:           const sessionFile = join(sessionsDir, sessionId, "session.yaml");
107:           if (existsSync(sessionFile)) {
108:             const content = readFileSync(sessionFile, "utf-8");
109:             const data = load(content) as SessionData;
110:             return {
111:               ...data,
112:               createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
113:               updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
114:             };
115:           }
116:         }
117:       }
118:     }
119: 
120:     return null;
121:   }
122: 
123:   async findByProjectAndId(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<Session | null> {
124:     const filePath = this.getSessionFilePath(projectId, sessionId);
125:     if (!existsSync(filePath)) {
126:       return null;
127:     }
128: 
129:     const content = readFileSync(filePath, "utf-8");
130:     const data = load(content) as SessionData;
131:     
132:     return {
133:       ...data,
134:       createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
135:       updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
136:     };
137:   }
138: 
139:   async listByProject(projectId: string): Promise<Session[]> {
140:     const sessionsDir = join(getPaths().projects, projectId, "sessions");
141:     if (!existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
142:       return [];
143:     }
144: 
145:     const entries = readdirSync(sessionsDir, { withFileTypes: true });
146:     const sessions: Session[] = [];
147: 
148:     for (const entry of entries) {
149:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
150:         const sessionFile = join(sessionsDir, entry.name, "session.yaml");
151:         if (existsSync(sessionFile)) {
152:           const content = readFileSync(sessionFile, "utf-8");
153:           const data = load(content) as SessionData;
154:           sessions.push({
155:             ...data,
156:             createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
157:             updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
158:           });
159:         }
160:       }
161:     }
162: 
163:     return sessions.sort((a, b) => b.createdAt.getTime() - a.createdAt.getTime());
164:   }
165: 
166:   async update(sessionId: string, updates: Partial<Omit<SessionData, "id" | "createdAt">>): Promise<Session | null> {
167:     const session = await this.findById(sessionId);
168:     if (!session) return null;
169: 
170:     const updatedData: SessionData = {
171:       ...session,
172:       ...updates,
173:       updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
174:     };
175: 
176:     const filePath = this.getSessionFilePath(session.projectId, sessionId);
177:     writeFileSync(filePath, dump(updatedData), "utf-8");
178: 
179:     return {
180:       ...updatedData,
181:       createdAt: new Date(updatedData.createdAt),
182:       updatedAt: new Date(updatedData.updatedAt),
183:     };
184:   }
185: 
186:   async delete(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<void> {
187:     const sessionPath = this.getSessionPath(projectId, sessionId);
188:     
189:     // Get session to find worktree path
190:     const session = await this.findByProjectAndId(projectId, sessionId);
191:     
192:     if (session && existsSync(session.worktreePath)) {
193:       // Delete worktree directory
194:       this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(session.worktreePath);
195:     }
196:     
197:     // Delete session directory
198:     if (existsSync(sessionPath)) {
199:       this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(sessionPath);
200:     }
201:   }
202: 
203:   private deleteDirectoryRecursive(dirPath: string): void {
204:     if (!existsSync(dirPath)) return;
205: 
206:     const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
207:     
208:     for (const entry of entries) {
209:       const entryPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
210:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
211:         this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(entryPath);
212:       } else {
213:         unlinkSync(entryPath);
214:       }
215:     }
216: 
217:     rmdirSync(dirPath);
218:   }
219: 
220:   async exists(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<boolean> {
221:     return existsSync(this.getSessionFilePath(projectId, sessionId));
222:   }
223: }

225: export const sessionRepository = new SessionRepository();

273: 
274:   // Scan filesystem directly for files
275:   const { readdirSync, statSync } = await import("fs");
276:   const { join, relative } = await import("path");
277:   
278:   const fileTree: { [key: string]: string[] } = {};
279:   
280:   function scanDir(dirPath: string, basePath: string) {
281:     if (!statSync(dirPath, { throwIfNoEntry: false })) {
282:       return;
283:     }
284:     
285:     const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
286:     
287:     for (const entry of entries) {
288:       const fullPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
289:       const relPath = relative(basePath, fullPath);
290:       
291:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
292:         scanDir(fullPath, basePath);
293:       } else {
294:         const parts = relPath.split("/");
295:         const fileName = parts.pop() || "";
296:         const dir = parts.length > 0 ? parts.join("/") : "(root)";
297:         
298:         if (!fileTree[dir]) {
299:           fileTree[dir] = [];
300:         }
301:         fileTree[dir].push(fileName);
302:       }
303:     }
304:   }
305:   
306:   try {
307:     scanDir(session.worktreePath, session.worktreePath);
308:   } catch (error) {
309:     console.error("Error scanning worktree:", error);
310:   }
311: 
312:   // Return HTML file tree
313:   let html = `<!DOCTYPE html>
314: <html>
315: <head><title>File Tree</title></head>
316: <body>
317: <div class="file-tree">
318: `;
319: 
320:   for (const [dir, files] of Object.entries(fileTree)) {
321:     html += `  <div class="dir">${dir}/</div>\n`;
322:     for (const file of files) {
323:       html += `    <div class="file">${file}</div>\n`;
324:     }
325:   }
326: 
327:   html += `</div>
328: </body>
329: </html>`;
330: 
331:   return c.html(html);
332: });

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/components/SessionDetailPage.tsx

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 00:19:12
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/components/SessionDetailPage.tsx

```
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/components/SessionDetailPage.tsx</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: import type { FC } from "hono/jsx";
2: import { Layout } from "./Layout.js";
3: 
4: interface Project {
5:   id: string;
6:   name: string;
7: }
8: 
9: interface Session {
10:   id: string;
11:   name: string;
12:   status: "active" | "paused" | "closed";
13:   worktreePath: string;
14:   createdAt: Date;
15: }
16: 
17: interface ChatMessage {
18:   role: "user" | "assistant" | "system";
19:   content: string;
20:   timestamp: string;
21: }
22: 
23: interface Agent {
24:   id: string;
25:   status: "starting" | "connected" | "failed" | "killed" | "died";
26:   pid?: number;
27:   startedAt: Date;
28: }
29: 
30: interface FileChange {
31:   path: string;
32:   status: "clean" | "modified" | "new" | "deleted" | "conflict";
33: }
34: 
35: interface SessionDetailProps {
36:   project: Project;
37:   session: Session;
38:   chatHistory: ChatMessage[];
39:   activeAgent?: Agent;
40:   changes?: FileChange[];
41:   hasConflicts?: boolean;
42: }
43: 
44: function renderFileTree(changes: FileChange[]) {
45:   // Group files by directory
46:   const fileTree: Map<string, { name: string; status: FileChange["status"] }[]> = new Map();
47:   
48:   for (const change of changes) {
49:     const parts = change.path.split("/");
50:     const fileName = parts.pop() || "";
51:     const dir = parts.length > 0 ? parts.join("/") : "(root)";
52:     
53:     if (!fileTree.has(dir)) {
54:       fileTree.set(dir, []);
55:     }
56:     fileTree.get(dir)!.push({ name: fileName, status: change.status });
57:   }
58:   
59:   // Sort directories
60:   const sortedDirs = Array.from(fileTree.entries()).sort((a, b) => a[0].localeCompare(b[0]));
61:   
62:   return (
63:     <div class="file-tree">
64:       {sortedDirs.map(([dir, files]) => (
65:         <div key={dir} class="file-tree-dir">
66:           <div class="file-tree-dir-name">{dir}/</div>
67:           <div class="file-tree-files">
68:             {files.map((file) => (
69:               <div key={file.name} class="file-tree-file">
70:                 <span class={`file-indicator file-indicator-${file.status}`}>
71:                   {file.status === "modified" && "[M]"}
72:                   {file.status === "new" && "[?]"}
73:                   {file.status === "deleted" && "[D]"}
74:                   {file.status === "conflict" && "[!]"}
75:                   {file.status === "clean" && "   "}
76:                 </span>
77:                 <span class={`file-name file-name-${file.status}`}>{file.name}</span>
78:               </div>
79:             ))}
80:           </div>
81:         </div>
82:       ))}
83:     </div>
84:   );
85: }
86: 
87: function getStatusIcon(status: FileChange["status"]): string {
88:   switch (status) {
89:     case "modified": return "M";
90:     case "new": return "?";
91:     case "deleted": return "D";
92:     case "conflict": return "!";
93:     default: return " ";
94:   }
95: }
96: 
97: export const SessionDetailPage: FC<SessionDetailProps> = ({
98:   project,
99:   session,
100:   chatHistory,
101:   activeAgent,
102:   changes = [],
103:   hasConflicts = false,
104: }) => {
105:   return (
106:     <Layout title={`${session.name} - ${project.name}`} showStatusLine={true} sessionId={session.id}>
107:       <div class="session-container">
108:         {/* Header */}
109:         <div class="session-header-bar">
110:           <div>
111:             <h1>{session.name}</h1>
112:             <span style="color: #888; font-size: 12px;">
113:               Project: {project.name} | Status: {session.status}
114:               {activeAgent && (
115:                 <span class={`agent-status agent-status-${activeAgent.status}`}>
116:                   | Agent: {activeAgent.status}
117:                   {activeAgent.pid && ` (PID: ${activeAgent.pid})`}
118:                 </span>
119:               )}
120:             </span>
121:           </div>
122:           <div style="display: flex; gap: 10px;">
123:             {activeAgent && (
124:               <form method="POST" action={`/agents/${activeAgent.id}/kill`}>
125:                 <button type="submit" class="btn-danger">Kill Agent</button>
126:               </form>
127:             )}
128:             {!activeAgent && (
129:               <form method="POST" action={`/sessions/${session.id}/agent`}>
130:                 <button type="submit" class="btn-primary">Start Agent</button>
131:               </form>
132:             )}
133:             <a href={`/sessions?projectId=${project.id}`} class="btn-secondary">
134:               Back to Sessions
135:             </a>
136:           </div>
137:         </div>
138: 
139:         {/* Three Buffer Layout */}
140:         <div class="buffers-container">

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 00:19:14)

Now I understand the current architecture. Let me visualize what the user wants:

**Current Flow:**
1. Session → "Start Agent" button spawns agent automatically
2. Agent is tied to session
3. User sees status but limited control

**Desired Flow:**
1. Agents are created/managed independently
2. When creating an agent → generates a token for the user to use externally
3. Creating a session → associate it with an existing agent
4. UI shows agent online/offline status, click for details (not to start)

This is a significant conceptual shift. The agent is no longer "spawned by the platform" but rather:
- User creates an agent record (generates token)
- User runs `mimo-agent --token=<generated-token>` on their own machine
- Agent connects back to platform
- Session is then associated with an agent

Let me explore more about what needs to change.

Interesting. Let me visualize the current vs desired architecture:

Let me look at how sessions currently track agents and what needs to change:

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/mimo-platform/proposal.md

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 00:19:27
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/mimo-platform/proposal.md

```
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/mimo-platform/proposal.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: # Proposal: mimo-platform
2: 
3: ## Why
4: 
5: Emacs is outdated for modern collaborative development. We need a web-based editor that combines the power of worktree-based development with AI agents, allowing users to chat with agents that code while maintaining full version control. Unlike traditional IDEs, this should be minimal, text-focused, and filesystem-driven—no databases, no bloat, just Emacs-style efficiency in the browser.
6: 
7: ## What Changes
8: 
9: - **New System**: Build mimo-platform using TypeScript/Bun with Elysia framework for minimal footprint
10: - **Auth System**: Simple username/password login/logout without email confirmation, stored in YAML files
11: - **Project Management**: Create projects, link to Git/Fossil repositories, switch between projects
12: - **Session Management**: Create sessions with titles that spawn worktrees, chat interface with streaming responses, file tree with change indicators, syntax-highlighted diffs
13: - **Agent Management**: Create agents that generate tokens, spawn mimo-agent processes that proxy ACP protocol, list active agents
14: - **VCS Integration**: Support both Git (native worktrees) and Fossil (virtual worktree via multiple clones), commit and push to remote
15: - **mimo-agent**: Build separate TypeScript/Bun single-file executable that connects via WebSocket, clones from Fossil server, proxies ACP, watches files, and reports changes
16: - **UI Style**: Emacs-inspired minimal interface with buffers, keybindings, split windows
17: 
18: ## Capabilities
19: 
20: ### New Capabilities
21: - `user-auth`: Simple username/password authentication, filesystem-based credential storage
22: - `project-management`: CRUD operations for projects, repository linking, project switching
23: - `session-management`: Session CRUD with worktree creation, chat with streaming, file viewing with syntax highlighting
24: - `agent-lifecycle`: Agent creation with token generation, process spawning, connection management
25: - `vcs-integration`: Git and Fossil repository support, worktree management, commit/push operations
26: - `file-sync`: Bidirectional file synchronization between agent worktree and original repository
27: 
28: ### Modified Capabilities
29: - None
30: 
31: ## Impact
32: 
33: - **New Dependencies**: Elixir/Phoenix, Hologram, Bun (for agent build), Fossil
34: - **Filesystem Structure**: Creates `~/.mimo/` directory structure for projects, sessions, and chat history
35: - **Network**: WebSocket connections between browser-platform-agent
36: - **Processes**: Fossil server per session, mimo-agent process per session
37: - **Distribution**: mimo-agent as separate downloadable binary

(End of file - total 37 lines)
</content>
```
## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 00:19:29)

Now I have a good understanding. Let me think through the user's desired changes:

1. **Current model:**
   - Sessions have agents spawned from within them
   - "Start Agent" button on session page
   - Platform spawns the mimo-agent process
   - Agent is tied to session creation time

2. **Desired model:**
   - Agents are created independently (on Agents page)
   - Creating agent generates a token
   - User manually starts mimo-agent with that token
   - Session creation associates with an agent (optional?)
   - UI shows agent online/offline status (not "Start Agent" button)
   - Clicking agent status shows details

Key questions the user might want to explore:

1. **Agent ownership model:**
   - Are agents per-user (user owns many agents)?
   - Or per-project?
   - Or per-session (but created independently)?

2. **Session-agent association:**
   - When creating a session, does user select an agent?
   - Or can any agent work with any session?
   - What happens if an agent is "offline" when session is created?

3. **Token lifecycle:**
   - Does creating agent show token once (like API keys)?
   - Or can user view token multiple times?
   - Token expiration?

4. **Agent "online" detection:**
   - WebSocket connection from agent to platform
   - Platform tracks active WebSocket connections
   - UI shows green/red indicator

5. **Delete agent:**
   - What happens to sessions that used this agent?
   - Is the association historical or active?

Let me present this analysis to the user and ask clarifying questions.

│                                  ┌──────────┐                          │
│                                  │ Associate│  ──▶ Select Agent ID     │
│                                  │  Agent   │                          │
│                                  └──────────┘                          │
│                                                                        │
└────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**Questions that emerge:**

1. **Agent ↔ Session relationship:**
   - Is this a **one-to-one** (agent is locked to one session)?
   - Or **one-to-many** (agent can serve multiple sessions over time)?
   - If one-to-one, what happens when session ends—agent freed or deleted?

2. **Agent creation timing:**
   - Can agents exist **without** a session? (just tokens waiting to be used)
   - Or must every agent be associated with a session at creation?

3. **"Online" status:**
   - Does the agent WebSocket connect to platform?
   - If so, platform tracks `activeConnections` (already exists in `service.ts:28`)
   - UI shows: 🟢 connected / 🔴 offline or disconnected

4. **Session creation flow:**
   ```
   Create Session form:
   ┌───────────────────────────────┐
   │ Name: [___________________]   │
   │                               │
   │ Agent: [Dropdown ▼]          │
   │        - Agent-001 (offline)  │
   │        - Agent-002 (online)   │
   │        - [Create New Agent]   │
   │                               │
   │ [Create Session]              │
   └───────────────────────────────┘
   ```
   - Or is agent optional (no agent assigned initially)?

5. **Token display:**
   - **One-time reveal** (like GitHub PATs—"copy now, won't show again")?
   - **Always visible** in agent details page?
   - **Regeneratable** (user can generate new token, old one invalidates)?

Looking at the current `AgentService.spawnAgent()`, it does:
- Create agent record
- Generate token
- **Spawn the process directly**
- Add PID tracking

The new model would split this: **create + token generation** stays, **spawn + PID tracking** goes away (user's responsibility).

What's your mental model for the agent-session relationship? And should tokens be one-time reveal or always visible?

## User (2026-04-04 00:21:19)

the agent-session is mimo-agent, this will connect to mimo-platform and will see the sessions that is responsabile, so it will proceed to clone the proxy repository and start the local agent like opencode or claude

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 00:21:21)

The user is clarifying the architecture. Let me understand:

1. `mimo-agent` is a separate process that the user runs locally
2. `mimo-agent` connects to `mimo-platform` via WebSocket (with token auth)
3. The agent receives session assignments from the platform
4. The agent handles:
   - Cloning/accessing the proxy repository (Fossil worktree)
   - Running local AI agent (opencode, claude, etc.) - the "ACP" (Agent Communication Protocol)
   - Watching files and reporting changes back to platform

So the flow is:

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                              NEW ARCHITECTURE                               │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                             │
│   USER FLOW:                                                                │
│                                                                             │
│   ┌──────────────┐    ┌──────────────┐    ┌──────────────────────────────┐ │
│   │ mimo-platform│    │  User        │    │       Local Machine          │ │
│   │              │    │  copies      │    │                              │ │
│   │ Create Agent │───▶│  token       │───▶│  mimo-agent --token=JWT      │ │
│   │ Get Token    │    │              │    │                              │ │
│   └──────────────┘    └──────────────┘    │       │                      │ │
│                                           │       │ connects via WS      │ │
│                                           │       ▼                      │ │
│                                           │  ┌─────────────┐             │ │
│                                           │  │ mimo-platform│◀──────────┼─┤
│                                           │  │ (WebSocket)  │            │ │
│                                           │  └─────────────┘             │ │
│                                           │       │                      │ │
│                                           │       │ assigns session      │ │
│                                           │       ▼                      │ │
│                                           │  ┌─────────────┐             │ │
│                                           │  │ Clone Proxy │             │ │
│                                           │  │ Repository  │             │ │
│                                           │  └──────┬──────┘             │ │
│                                           │         │                    │ │
│                                           │         ▼                    │ │
│                                           │  ┌─────────────┐             │ │
│                                           │  │ Run ACP     │             │ │
│                                           │  │ (opencode/  │             │ │
│                                           │  │  claude)    │             │ │
│                                           │  └─────────────┘             │ │
│                                           └──────────────────────────────┘ │
│                                                                             │
│   SESSION FLOW:                                                             │
│                                                                             │
│   ┌──────────────┐    ┌──────────────┐                                     │
│   │ Create       │    │ Session.yaml │                                     │
│   │ Session      │───▶│ assignedAgent│                                     │
│   │              │    │   : agent-id │                                     │
│   └──────────────┘    └──────────────┘                                     │
│                                                                             │
│   AGENT:                    SESSION:                                        │
│   - id                      - id                                            │
│   - token                   - name                                          │
│   - owner                   - projectId                                     │
│   - status (online/offline) - assignedAgentId  ◀── NEW FIELD              │
│   - createdAt               - worktreePath                                  │
│              │                                                              │
│              │ (no sessionId - agent can handle multiple sessions)         │
│              │                                                              │
│              └──▶ Agent is INDEPENDENT of sessions                         │
│                                                                             │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

So the key insight:

1. **Agent is independent** - created separately from sessions
2. **Agent sees sessions assigned to it** - platform sends session list to connected agent
3. **Agent runs ACP locally** - opencode, claude, whatever local AI agent
4. **Session has `assignedAgentId`** not the other way around

This flips the ownership:
- OLD: Agent belongs to Session (`agent.sessionId`)
- NEW: Session belongs to Agent (`session.assignedAgentId`)

Or maybe:
- Agent has NO reference to session
- Session has reference to Agent
- Multiple sessions can reference same agent (one at a time? or concurrently?)

Let me clarify further with the user about:
1. Can one agent serve multiple sessions concurrently?
2. Or is it one session at a time?
3. When agent connects, does it "claim" its sessions?

**Key questions:**

1. **Session assignment:**
   - When creating a session, user picks from dropdown of their agents?
   - Or can session exist without agent (agent-assigned-later)?

2. **One agent, multiple sessions:**
   - Can one mimo-agent serve multiple sessions?
   - Or is it `one agent = one active session` at a time?

3. **Agent "online" detection:**
   Platform already tracks `activeConnections: Map<string, WebSocket>` in service.
   When agent connects with token, platform validates → marks agent online.
   On disconnect → marks offline.

4. **The agent sees its sessions:**
   ```
   Agent connects ──▶ Platform validates token
                    ──▶ Platform finds sessions WHERE assignedAgentId = agent.id
                    ──▶ Sends session list to agent
                    ──▶ Agent clones proxy repo for each session?
                        Or works on ONE session at a time?
   ```

5. **Token visibility:**
   - One-time reveal (show once, then never again)?
   - Or always visible in agent detail page?
   - Can regenerate?

What's your mental model for: one agent serving multiple sessions vs one-at-a-time?

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 00:23:37)

Now I have a clear picture. Let me summarize the key changes:

1. **Agent creation is independent** - users create agents in the UI, get a token, run mimo-agent themselves
2. **Session assigns agent from dropdown** - session has `assignedAgentId`
3. **One agent manages multiple sessions** - agent can clone multiple worktrees and spawn multiple ACP processes
4. **Agent "online" status** - tracked via WebSocket connection, not PID tracking
5. **Token always visible** - user can always see the token in agent details page, cannot regenerate

Let me think about what needs to change:

**Database/Data structure changes:**

1. `Agent` schema changes:
   - Remove `sessionId` (agent no longer owned by session)
   - Remove `pid` (platform doesn't spawn, doesn't track PID)
   - Keep `owner`, `token`, `status`, `startedAt`, `lastActivityAt`

2. `Session` schema changes:
   - Add `assignedAgentId` (optional, references agent)

3. `AgentService` changes:
   - Remove `spawnAgent` - replace with `createAgent` (just creates record + token)
   - Remove process spawning logic
   - Remove PID tracking
   - Keep `handleAgentConnect`, `handleAgentDisconnect` for WebSocket
   - Remove `killAgent` - or change to "mark as killed" (but user controls lifecycle)
   - Keep `activeConnections` map for tracking online status

4. `AgentRepository` changes:
   - Remove `findBySessionId` - agents no longer belong to sessions
   - Add `findOnlineAgents()` or similar for listing agents by status

5. UI changes:
   - Agents page: Create/List/Delete agents, show online status, show token
   - Session create page: Dropdown to select agent
   - Session detail page: Show agent status badge (click for details), no "Start Agent" button
   
6. Spec changes:
   - `agent-lifecycle/spec.md` needs updating to reflect user-spawned agents with independent management, while `session-management/spec.md` now includes agent selection from a dropdown and tracks `assignedAgentId`. The core shift is decoupling agent lifecycle from sessions—agents exist independently, connect on their own, and sessions simply reference them by assignment rather than ownership.

The `Agent` data structure still needs `sessionId` and `projectId` for now, but these references should move once the service layer is refactored to handle agent discovery independently.

**Summary of changes needed:**

| Layer | Current | New |
|-------|---------|-----|
| **Agent schema** | `sessionId`, `projectId`, `pid` | Remove these, keep `owner`, `token`, `status` |
| **Session schema** | No agent reference | Add `assignedAgentId?: string` |
| **AgentService** | `spawnAgent()` spawns process | `createAgent()` just creates token |
| **AgentService** | `killAgent()`, PID tracking | Remove or simplify |
| **AgentService** | Tracks `activeConnections` | Keep, use for "online" status |
| **UI: Agents page** | Lists agents with Kill/Retry | Create/Delete, show online/offline |
| **UI: Session create** | No agent dropdown | Add agent dropdown |
| **UI: Session detail** | "Start Agent" button | Show agent badge, click for details |
| **Spec** | Agent lifecycle in platform context | Agent lifecycle is user-controlled |

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 00:25:08)

Good - there's an existing `agent-lifecycle` spec in the mimo-platform change. This refactor will modify that capability. Let me create the proposal.

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/refactor-agent-lifecycle/proposal.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 00:25:14
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/refactor-agent-lifecycle/proposal.md
content: ## Why

The current agent lifecycle model ties agents to sessions at creation time, with the platform spawning and managing the mimo-agent process. This creates an inverted ownership model where the platform manages process lifecycle instead of the user. Users need to create agents independently, receive a token, and run mimo-agent locally—allowing one agent to manage multiple sessions in parallel, each with its own ACP process (opencode, claude, etc.).

## What Changes

- **BREAKING**: Remove platform-spawned agent processes—users now run `mimo-agent --token=XXX` locally
- **BREAKING**: Remove `sessionId` and `projectId` from Agent schema—agents are no longer bound to sessions at creation
- **BREAKING**: Remove `pid` tracking from Agent schema—platform no longer manages process lifecycle
- Add `assignedAgentId` to Session schema—sessions reference agents instead of agents owning sessions
- Add `status: "online" | "offline"` to Agent—derived from WebSocket connection state
- Add agent creation UI—create agent, receive token (always visible, cannot regenerate)
- Add agent dropdown in session creation—associate existing agent with session
- Add agent detail view—show status, token, sessions using this agent
- Remove "Start Agent" button from session detail—replace with agent status badge that shows details on click

## Capabilities

### New Capabilities
- `agent-management`: CRUD operations for agents independent of sessions, token generation (one-time view, always visible), online/offline status tracking via WebSocket

### Modified Capabilities
- `agent-lifecycle`: Remove platform-spawned process management, agent now connects to platform with token, one agent can serve multiple sessions in parallel
- `session-management`: Add agent assignment via dropdown on session creation, session references agent via `assignedAgentId`

## Impact

- **Agent schema**: Remove `sessionId`, `projectId`, `pid`; agent is now independent entity
- **Session schema**: Add `assignedAgentId` (optional foreign key to agent)
- **AgentService**: Remove `spawnAgent()`, `killAgent()`, PID tracking; keep `createAgent()` with token generation and `handleAgentConnect()`/`handleAgentDisconnect()` for status
- **AgentRepository**: Remove session-scoped queries; add `findByStatus()` for online/offline listing
- **UI: Agents page**: Create/Delete agents, show online/offline status, display token in detail view
- **UI: Session create form**: Add agent dropdown populated from user's agents
- **UI: Session detail page**: Remove "Start Agent" button, add agent status badge with detail modal
- **mimo-agent**: Already designed to connect with token—no changes needed, just receives token from user

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/refactor-agent-lifecycle/design.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 00:25:34
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/refactor-agent-lifecycle/design.md
content: ## Context

The current architecture has the platform spawn and manage mimo-agent processes, binding agents to sessions at creation time. This inverts ownership—users cannot run agents locally, cannot manage multiple sessions with one agent, and cannot see tokens after creation. The refactored architecture moves agent ownership to the user: they create agents (receive tokens), run mimo-agent locally with that token, and agents connect back to the platform to discover their assigned sessions.

Current state:
- Agent schema: `{id, sessionId, projectId, owner, token, status, pid, startedAt, lastActivityAt}`
- AgentService: `spawnAgent()` spawns process, `killAgent()` terminates, tracks PIDs
- Session creation: No agent selection—agent spawned via "Start Agent" button
- Session detail: "Start Agent" button spawns agent on-demand

Target state:
- Agent schema: `{id, owner, token, status, startedAt, lastActivityAt}`
- Session schema: Add `assignedAgentId`
- AgentService: `createAgent()` generates token, `handleAgentConnect()`/`handleAgentDisconnect()` for status
- Session creation: Agent dropdown selects from user's agents
- Session detail: Agent status badge, click for details (no spawn button)

## Goals / Non-Goals

**Goals:**
- Separate agent lifecycle from session lifecycle
- Allow users to create agents and receive tokens
- Allow one agent to serve multiple sessions in parallel
- Track agent online/offline status via WebSocket connection state
- Show agent token in UI (always visible, cannot regenerate)

**Non-Goals:**
- Token regeneration or revocation (out of scope)
- Agent-to-agent communication (out of scope)
- Multi-tenant agent sharing (agent belongs to one owner)

## Decisions

### Agent Ownership Model
**Decision**: Agent is independent entity owned by user, not bound to session at creation.

**Rationale**: 
- Previous model: Agent created when session starts, bound to that session
- New model: Agent created independently, associated with sessions via `assignedAgentId`
- Allows user to run one mimo-agent that manages multiple sessions simultaneously
- Cleaner separation: user controls agent process, platform just tracks connection state

**Alternatives considered**:
- Embed agent ID in session creation form (chosen)
- Auto-assign agent on first connection (rejected: less explicit, harder to track)

### Session-Agent Association
**Decision**: Session has optional `assignedAgentId` foreign key to agent.

**Rationale**:
- Session may exist without agent temporarily (agent not yet created)
- Agent can view which sessions it's responsible for via query
- Many sessions can reference same agent (parallel work)

**Alternatives considered**:
- Agent stores array of session IDs (rejected: harder to query, sync issues)
- Bidirectional reference (rejected: unnecessary complexity)

### Status Tracking
**Decision**: Agent's `status` derived from WebSocket connection state.

**Rationale**:
- Platform already tracks `activeConnections: Map<string, WebSocket>` in AgentService
- On connect: mark agent "online"
- On disconnect: mark agent "offline"
- No polling required—status is event-driven

### Token Visibility
**Decision**: Token always visible in agent detail, never regenerated.

**Rationale**:
- Simplicity: no token versioning, no revocation logic
- User copies token once after creation, or revisits page to copy again
- If compromised, user deletes agent and creates new one

## Risks / Trade-offs

| Risk | Mitigation |
|------|------------|
| Token exposed in UI | Token is single-secret; users should treat like password. Future: add expiration or regeneration. |
| Agent disconnects unexpectedly | Status shows "offline"; user can restart mimo-agent locally |
| Session has no agent assigned | Optional field; session creation form allows "None" or agent creation inline |
| Multiple agents, user confusion | UI shows agent details; sessions list which agent is assigned |
| Orphaned agents (user forgets) | Agent list with "delete" option; owners can clean up |

```
Wrote file successfully.

│ changes │
╰─────────╯

@@ -0,0 +1,84 @@
+## Context
+
+The current architecture has the platform spawn and manage mimo-agent processes, binding agents to sessions at creation time. This inverts ownership—users cannot run agents locally, cannot manage multiple sessions with one agent, and cannot see tokens after creation. The refactored architecture moves agent ownership to the user: they create agents (receive tokens), run mimo-agent locally with that token, and agents connect back to the platform to discover their assigned sessions.
+
+Current state:
+- Agent schema: `{id, sessionId, projectId, owner, token, status, pid, startedAt, lastActivityAt}`
+- AgentService: `spawnAgent()` spawns process, `killAgent()` terminates, tracks PIDs
+- Session creation: No agent selection—agent spawned via "Start Agent" button
+- Session detail: "Start Agent" button spawns agent on-demand
+
+Target state:
+- Agent schema: `{id, owner, token, status, startedAt, lastActivityAt}`
+- Session schema: Add `assignedAgentId`
+- AgentService: `createAgent()` generates token, `handleAgentConnect()`/`handleAgentDisconnect()` for status
+- Session creation: Agent dropdown selects from user's agents
+- Session detail: Agent status badge, click for details (no spawn button)
+
+## Goals / Non-Goals
+
+**Goals:**
+- Separate agent lifecycle from session lifecycle
+- Allow users to create agents and receive tokens
+- Allow one agent to serve multiple sessions in parallel
+- Track agent online/offline status via WebSocket connection state
+- Show agent token in UI (always visible, cannot regenerate)
+
+**Non-Goals:**
+- Token regeneration or revocation (out of scope)
+- Agent-to-agent communication (out of scope)
+- Multi-tenant agent sharing (agent belongs to one owner)
+
+## Decisions
+
+### Agent Ownership Model
+**Decision**: Agent is independent entity owned by user, not bound to session at creation.
+
+**Rationale**: 
+- Previous model: Agent created when session starts, bound to that session
+- New model: Agent created independently, associated with sessions via `assignedAgentId`
+- Allows user to run one mimo-agent that manages multiple sessions simultaneously
+- Cleaner separation: user controls agent process, platform just tracks connection state
+
+**Alternatives considered**:
+- Embed agent ID in session creation form (chosen)
+- Auto-assign agent on first connection (rejected: less explicit, harder to track)
+
+### Session-Agent Association
+**Decision**: Session has optional `assignedAgentId` foreign key to agent.
+
+**Rationale**:
+- Session may exist without agent temporarily (agent not yet created)
+- Agent can view which sessions it's responsible for via query
+- Many sessions can reference same agent (parallel work)
+
+**Alternatives considered**:
+- Agent stores array of session IDs (rejected: harder to query, sync issues)
+- Bidirectional reference (rejected: unnecessary complexity)
+
+### Status Tracking
+**Decision**: Agent's `status` derived from WebSocket connection state.
+
+**Rationale**:
+- Platform already tracks `activeConnections: Map<string, WebSocket>` in AgentService
+- On connect: mark agent "online"
+- On disconnect: mark agent "offline"
+- No polling required—status is event-driven
+
+### Token Visibility
+**Decision**: Token always visible in agent detail, never regenerated.
+
+**Rationale**:
+- Simplicity: no token versioning, no revocation logic
+- User copies token once after creation, or revisits page to copy again
+- If compromised, user deletes agent and creates new one
+
+## Risks / Trade-offs
+
+| Risk | Mitigation |
+|------|------------|
+| Token exposed in UI | Token is single-secret; users should treat like password. Future: add expiration or regeneration. |
+| Agent disconnects unexpectedly | Status shows "offline"; user can restart mimo-agent locally |
+| Session has no agent assigned | Optional field; session creation form allows "None" or agent creation inline |
+| Multiple agents, user confusion | UI shows agent details; sessions list which agent is assigned |
+| Orphaned agents (user forgets) | Agent list with "delete" option; owners can clean up |
\ No newline at end of file
